security: [ { bearerAuth: [] } ]

1. Realtime protocol and message shapes (condensed)


* Transport: WebSocket /ws (JSON). SSE fallback: GET /sse (server push) + REST POST for send.
* At-least-once delivery. Client supplies idempotencyKey; server echoes it.

Client → Server

* client.message.send { roomId, body? | ciphertext?, idempotencyKey }
* client.canvas.patch { canvasId, patch, baseVersion }
* client.rule.create { roomId, when, then }
* client.typing { roomId, state }
* resume { lastCursor }

Server → Client

* server.welcome { sessionId, heartbeatSec }
* server.message.created { message, cursor }
* server.canvas.updated { canvasId, patch, version }
* server.rule.fired { ruleId, summary }
* server.timecapsule.unlocked { roomId, message }

Rule JSON (MVP)

* when: { contains:"#todo" } or { mention:"@urgent" }
* then: [ { add_task:{ title:"Auto: ${message}" } }, { pin_message:{} } ]


1. Backend (trimmed, runnable excerpts)

SecurityConfig.java (permit dev login header; JWT optional)
javaDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
package com.oc.config;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.*;
import org.springframework.security.config.annotation.web.reactive.EnableWebFluxSecurity;
import org.springframework.security.config.web.server.ServerHttpSecurity;
import org.springframework.security.web.server.SecurityWebFilterChain;
@Configuration @EnableWebFluxSecurity
public class SecurityConfig {
  @Bean SecurityWebFilterChain chain(ServerHttpSecurity http) {
    return http.csrf(csrf->csrf.disable())
      .authorizeExchange(e->e.pathMatchers("/actuator/","/ws","/sse").permitAll().anyExchange().permitAll())
      .build(); // keep simple for MVP; swap to JWT in prod
  }
}
RealtimeHandler.java (core send + broadcast + rule hook)
javaDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
package com.oc.ws;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.oc.domain.Message;
import com.oc.repo.MessageRepo;
import com.oc.rules.RuleEngine;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
import org.springframework.web.reactive.socket.*;
import reactor.core.publisher.*;
import java.util.Map;
@Component
public class RealtimeHandler implements WebSocketHandler {
  private final ObjectMapper om = new ObjectMapper();
  private final Sinks.Many<String> bus = Sinks.many().multicast().onBackpressureBuffer();
  private final MessageRepo messages; private final RuleEngine rules;
  public RealtimeHandler(MessageRepo m, RuleEngine r){ this.messages=m; this.rules=r; }
  @Override public Mono<Void> handle(WebSocketSession s) {
    var in = s.receive().map(WebSocketMessage::getPayloadAsText).flatMap(txt -> {
      try { var e = om.readValue(txt, Map.class);
        if ("client.message.send".equals(e.get("type"))) {
          var m = Message.create(e); messages.save(m); rules.onMessageCreated(m);
          bus.tryEmitNext(om.writeValueAsString(Map.of("type","server.message.created","message",m)));
        }
      } catch(Exception ignore){}
      return Mono.empty();
    });
    var out = bus.asFlux().map(s::textMessage)
      .mergeWith(Mono.just(s.textMessage("{\"type\":\"server.welcome\",\"heartbeatSec\":25}")));
    return s.send(out).and(in);
  }
}
RuleEngine.java (WHEN contains -> THEN add_task)
javaDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
package com.oc.rules;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.*;
import com.oc.domain.*;
import com.oc.repo.*;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
@Service
public class RuleEngine {
  private final RuleRepo rr; private final CanvasRepo cr; private final ObjectMapper om = new ObjectMapper();
  public RuleEngine(RuleRepo rr, CanvasRepo cr){ this.rr=rr; this.cr=cr; }
  public void onMessageCreated(Message m){
    rr.findByRoomId(m.getRoomId()).forEach(r -> {
      try {
        var when = om.readTree(r.getWhenJson()); var then = om.readTree(r.getThenJson());
        if (matches(when, m.getBody())) apply(then, m);
      } catch(Exception ignore){}
    });
  }
  private boolean matches(JsonNode w, String body){ if (body==null) return false;
    if (w.has("contains")) return body.contains(w.get("contains").asText());
    if (w.has("mention")) return body.contains(w.get("mention").asText());
    return false;
  }
  private void apply(JsonNode t, Message m){
    if (t.isArray()) t.forEach(n->apply(n,m));
    else if (t.has("add_task")) cr.addTask(m.getRoomId(), m.getBody());
    else if (t.has("pin_message")) m.setPinned(true);
  }
}
TimeCapsuleService.java (time and reaction unlock, minimal)
javaDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
package com.oc.timecapsules;
import com.oc.repo.TimeCapsuleRepo; import com.oc.domain.TimeCapsule;
import org.springframework.scheduling.annotation.Scheduled; import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
import java.time.Instant;
@Service
public class TimeCapsuleService {
  private final TimeCapsuleRepo repo;
  public TimeCapsuleService(TimeCapsuleRepo r){ this.repo=r; }
  @Scheduled(fixedDelay = 60000)
  public void tick(){
    var now = Instant.now();
    repo.findLockable(now).forEach(tc -> { tc.setUnlockedAt(now); repo.save(tc); /* emit system message */});
  }
  public void onReactionAdded(java.util.UUID messageId){
    repo.findByMessageId(messageId).ifPresent(tc -> {
      if (repo.reactionCount(messageId) >= tc.getMinReactions()) { tc.setUnlockedAt(Instant.now()); repo.save(tc); }
    });
  }
}
S3 presign controller (unchanged pattern, few lines)
javaDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
package com.oc.storage;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.*; record PresignReq(String key,String mime){} record PresignRes(String putUrl,String getUrl){}
@RestController @RequestMapping("/files")
public class S3Controller {
  @PostMapping("/presign") public PresignRes presign(@RequestBody PresignReq r){
    return new PresignRes("http://minio/put/"+r.key(),"http://minio/get/"+r.key()); // stub for MVP; swap to AWS SDK in prod
  }
}

1. Frontend (tiny but functional)

State store with offline queue
tsDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
// apps/web/src/state/store.ts
import create from 'zustand';
type Q = { id:string; roomId:string; body?:string; ciphertext?:string; idem:string };
export const useStore = create<any>(()=>({ rooms:[], messages:{}, queue:[] }));
export const addMessage = (roomId:string, msg:any) =>
  useStore.setState((s:any)=>({ messages:{...s.messages, [roomId]:[...(s.messages[roomId]||[]), msg] }}));
export const enqueue = (q:Q)=>useStore.setState((s:any)=>({ queue:[...s.queue,q] }));
export const dequeue = (id:string)=>useStore.setState((s:any)=>({ queue:s.queue.filter((x:Q)=>x.id!==id) }));
WebSocket client with resume + queue flush
tsDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
// apps/web/src/ws/realtime.ts
import { addMessage, enqueue, dequeue, useStore } from '../state/store';
let ws:WebSocket|undefined; let lastCursor:string|null=null;
export function connect(){ ws = new WebSocket(ws://${location.hostname}:8080/ws);
  ws.onopen = () => flush(); ws.onmessage = e => { const evt = JSON.parse(e.data);
    if (evt.type==='server.message.created') addMessage(evt.message.roomId, evt.message);
  }; ws.onclose = () => setTimeout(connect, 800);
}
export function sendOrQueue(payload:any){ try{ ws?.send(JSON.stringify(payload)); }catch{ enqueue({ id:payload.idempotencyKey, roomId:payload.roomId, body:payload.body, ciphertext:payload.ciphertext, idem:payload.idempotencyKey }); } }
function flush(){ for(const q of useStore.getState().queue) { ws?.send(JSON.stringify({ type:'client.message.send', roomId:q.roomId, body:q.body, ciphertext:q.ciphertext, idempotencyKey:q.idem })); dequeue(q.id); } }
E2EE helpers (sealed box via libsodium-wrappers; minimal)
tsDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
// apps/web/src/e2ee/crypto.ts
import sodium from 'libsodium-wrappers-sumo';
export async function ensureKeys(){
  await sodium.ready;
  const s = localStorage.getItem('dmKeys'); if (s) return JSON.parse(s);
  const kp = sodium.crypto_box_keypair();
  const keys = { pub: sodium.to_base64(kp.publicKey), sec: sodium.to_base64(kp.privateKey) };
  localStorage.setItem('dmKeys', JSON.stringify(keys)); return keys;
}
export async function encryptFor(pubB64:string, text:string){
  await sodium.ready; return sodium.to_base64(sodium.crypto_box_seal(new TextEncoder().encode(text), sodium.from_base64(pubB64)));
}
export async function decryptFrom(cipherB64:string){
  await sodium.ready; const { pub, sec } = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('dmKeys')!);
  const m = sodium.crypto_box_seal_open(sodium.from_base64(cipherB64), sodium.from_base64(pub), sodium.from_base64(sec));
  return new TextDecoder().decode(m);
}
Minimal Rule Editor (WHEN contains → THEN add_task)
tsxDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
// apps/web/src/rules/RuleEditor.tsx
import React,{useState} from 'react';
export default function RuleEditor({roomId}:{roomId:string}) {
  const [contains,setContains]=useState('#todo');
  async function save(){
    await fetch(/rooms/${roomId}/rules, { method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify({ when_json:{contains}, then_json:[{add_task:{title:'Auto'}}] })});
    alert('Rule saved');
  }
  return <div><input value={contains} onChange={e=>setContains(e.target.value)}/><button onClick={save}>Save</button></div>;
}

export default function Tasks({canvas}:{canvas:any}) {

}

2. 
Architecture diagram (compact) + explanation
+--------------------+     WS/SSE     +----------------------+
| React PWA (Vite)   |<-------------->| Spring Boot WebFlux  |
| - Rooms/Messages   |                | - REST + WebSocket   |
| - Rule Editor      |                | - Rules Engine (MVP) |
| - Canvases (3)     |                | - Time Capsules      |
| - E2EE in browser  |                | - Presign S3         |
| - IndexedDB queue  |                | - Prometheus/Otel    |
+--------------------+                +-----+-----------+----+
| REST                               |           |
v                                     v           v
Web Push/SW                             Postgres      Redis
(core data)   (presence/pubsub)
Explanation



* WebSocket for realtime; SSE fallback.
* Offline queue flushes on reconnect with idempotency keys.
* E2EE DMs: client encrypts; server stores ciphertext only.

Database schema and Flyway migrations (first migration)
Essential tables only (presence history omitted to stay small; live presence via Redis).


sqlDownloadCopy code Wrap-- Author: Ritika Singh
-- apps/api/src/main/resources/db/migration/V1__init.sql
CREATE TYPE room_type AS ENUM ('dm','group');
CREATE TYPE role_type AS ENUM ('owner','admin','member');
CREATE TYPE canvas_type AS ENUM ('tasks','poll','whiteboard');

CREATE TABLE users (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  handle TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
  display_name TEXT NOT NULL,
  email TEXT UNIQUE,
  dm_public_key BYTEA,       -- for E2EE DMs (optional)
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

CREATE TABLE rooms (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  type room_type NOT NULL,
  name TEXT,
  created_by UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

CREATE TABLE memberships (
  user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  room_id UUID REFERENCES rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  role role_type NOT NULL,
  joined_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  PRIMARY KEY (user_id, room_id)
);

CREATE TABLE messages (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  room_id UUID REFERENCES rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  sender_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  body TEXT,
  body_ciphertext BYTEA,
  attachments JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT '[]',
  idempotency_key TEXT UNIQUE,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

CREATE TABLE rules (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  room_id UUID REFERENCES rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  when_json JSONB NOT NULL,
  then_json JSONB NOT NULL,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

CREATE TABLE canvases (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  room_id UUID REFERENCES rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  type canvas_type NOT NULL,
  data_json JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
  updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

CREATE TABLE reactions (
  message_id UUID REFERENCES messages(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  emoji TEXT NOT NULL,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  PRIMARY KEY (message_id, user_id, emoji)
);

CREATE TABLE time_capsules (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  room_id UUID REFERENCES rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  payload_json JSONB NOT NULL,             -- message to emit
  unlock_at TIMESTAMPTZ,                   -- time-based
  min_reactions INT,                       -- reaction-based
  message_id UUID,                         -- optional: associated message to watch
  unlocked_at TIMESTAMPTZ
);

-- FTS for searchable (non-E2EE) messages
CREATE MATERIALIZED VIEW fts_messages AS
SELECT id, room_id, to_tsvector('english', coalesce(body,'')) AS tsv
FROM messages WHERE body IS NOT NULL;
CREATE UNIQUE INDEX fts_messages_pk ON fts_messages (id);
CREATE INDEX fts_messages_tsv_idx ON fts_messages USING GIN (tsv);

    post: { summary: Set my public key (base64) }
  /dm-keys/{userId}:
    get: { summary: Get user’s public key }

  /files/presign: { post: { summary: S3 presigned URLs } }

security: [ { bearerAuth: [] } ]

1. Realtime protocol and message shapes (condensed)


* Transport: WebSocket /ws (JSON). SSE fallback: GET /sse (server push) + REST POST for send.
* At-least-once delivery. Client supplies idempotencyKey; server echoes it.

Client → Server

* client.message.send { roomId, body? | ciphertext?, idempotencyKey }
* client.canvas.patch { canvasId, patch, baseVersion }
* client.rule.create { roomId, when, then }
* client.typing { roomId, state }
* resume { lastCursor }

Server → Client

* server.welcome { sessionId, heartbeatSec }
* server.message.created { message, cursor }
* server.canvas.updated { canvasId, patch, version }
* server.rule.fired { ruleId, summary }
* server.timecapsule.unlocked { roomId, message }

Rule JSON (MVP)

* when: { contains:"#todo" } or { mention:"@urgent" }
* then: [ { add_task:{ title:"Auto: ${message}" } }, { pin_message:{} } ]


1. Backend (trimmed, runnable excerpts)

SecurityConfig.java (permit dev login header; JWT optional)
javaDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
package com.oc.config;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.*;
import org.springframework.security.config.annotation.web.reactive.EnableWebFluxSecurity;
import org.springframework.security.config.web.server.ServerHttpSecurity;
import org.springframework.security.web.server.SecurityWebFilterChain;
@Configuration @EnableWebFluxSecurity
public class SecurityConfig {
  @Bean SecurityWebFilterChain chain(ServerHttpSecurity http) {
    return http.csrf(csrf->csrf.disable())
      .authorizeExchange(e->e.pathMatchers("/actuator/","/ws","/sse").permitAll().anyExchange().permitAll())
      .build(); // keep simple for MVP; swap to JWT in prod
  }
}
RealtimeHandler.java (core send + broadcast + rule hook)
javaDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
package com.oc.ws;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.oc.domain.Message;
import com.oc.repo.MessageRepo;
import com.oc.rules.RuleEngine;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
import org.springframework.web.reactive.socket.*;
import reactor.core.publisher.*;
import java.util.Map;
@Component
public class RealtimeHandler implements WebSocketHandler {
  private final ObjectMapper om = new ObjectMapper();
  private final Sinks.Many<String> bus = Sinks.many().multicast().onBackpressureBuffer();
  private final MessageRepo messages; private final RuleEngine rules;
  public RealtimeHandler(MessageRepo m, RuleEngine r){ this.messages=m; this.rules=r; }
  @Override public Mono<Void> handle(WebSocketSession s) {
    var in = s.receive().map(WebSocketMessage::getPayloadAsText).flatMap(txt -> {
      try { var e = om.readValue(txt, Map.class);
        if ("client.message.send".equals(e.get("type"))) {
          var m = Message.create(e); messages.save(m); rules.onMessageCreated(m);
          bus.tryEmitNext(om.writeValueAsString(Map.of("type","server.message.created","message",m)));
        }
      } catch(Exception ignore){}
      return Mono.empty();
    });
    var out = bus.asFlux().map(s::textMessage)
      .mergeWith(Mono.just(s.textMessage("{\"type\":\"server.welcome\",\"heartbeatSec\":25}")));
    return s.send(out).and(in);
  }
}
RuleEngine.java (WHEN contains -> THEN add_task)
javaDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
package com.oc.rules;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.*;
import com.oc.domain.*;
import com.oc.repo.*;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
@Service
public class RuleEngine {
  private final RuleRepo rr; private final CanvasRepo cr; private final ObjectMapper om = new ObjectMapper();
  public RuleEngine(RuleRepo rr, CanvasRepo cr){ this.rr=rr; this.cr=cr; }
  public void onMessageCreated(Message m){
    rr.findByRoomId(m.getRoomId()).forEach(r -> {
      try {
        var when = om.readTree(r.getWhenJson()); var then = om.readTree(r.getThenJson());
        if (matches(when, m.getBody())) apply(then, m);
      } catch(Exception ignore){}
    });
  }
  private boolean matches(JsonNode w, String body){ if (body==null) return false;
    if (w.has("contains")) return body.contains(w.get("contains").asText());
    if (w.has("mention")) return body.contains(w.get("mention").asText());
    return false;
  }
  private void apply(JsonNode t, Message m){
    if (t.isArray()) t.forEach(n->apply(n,m));
    else if (t.has("add_task")) cr.addTask(m.getRoomId(), m.getBody());
    else if (t.has("pin_message")) m.setPinned(true);
  }
}
TimeCapsuleService.java (time and reaction unlock, minimal)
javaDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
package com.oc.timecapsules;
import com.oc.repo.TimeCapsuleRepo; import com.oc.domain.TimeCapsule;
import org.springframework.scheduling.annotation.Scheduled; import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
import java.time.Instant;
@Service
public class TimeCapsuleService {
  private final TimeCapsuleRepo repo;
  public TimeCapsuleService(TimeCapsuleRepo r){ this.repo=r; }
  @Scheduled(fixedDelay = 60000)
  public void tick(){
    var now = Instant.now();
    repo.findLockable(now).forEach(tc -> { tc.setUnlockedAt(now); repo.save(tc); /* emit system message */});
  }
  public void onReactionAdded(java.util.UUID messageId){
    repo.findByMessageId(messageId).ifPresent(tc -> {
      if (repo.reactionCount(messageId) >= tc.getMinReactions()) { tc.setUnlockedAt(Instant.now()); repo.save(tc); }
    });
  }
}
S3 presign controller (unchanged pattern, few lines)
javaDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
package com.oc.storage;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.*; record PresignReq(String key,String mime){} record PresignRes(String putUrl,String getUrl){}
@RestController @RequestMapping("/files")
public class S3Controller {
  @PostMapping("/presign") public PresignRes presign(@RequestBody PresignReq r){
    return new PresignRes("http://minio/put/"+r.key(),"http://minio/get/"+r.key()); // stub for MVP; swap to AWS SDK in prod
  }
}

1. Frontend (tiny but functional)

State store with offline queue
tsDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
// apps/web/src/state/store.ts
import create from 'zustand';
type Q = { id:string; roomId:string; body?:string; ciphertext?:string; idem:string };
export const useStore = create<any>(()=>({ rooms:[], messages:{}, queue:[] }));
export const addMessage = (roomId:string, msg:any) =>
  useStore.setState((s:any)=>({ messages:{...s.messages, [roomId]:[...(s.messages[roomId]||[]), msg] }}));
export const enqueue = (q:Q)=>useStore.setState((s:any)=>({ queue:[...s.queue,q] }));
export const dequeue = (id:string)=>useStore.setState((s:any)=>({ queue:s.queue.filter((x:Q)=>x.id!==id) }));
WebSocket client with resume + queue flush
tsDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
// apps/web/src/ws/realtime.ts
import { addMessage, enqueue, dequeue, useStore } from '../state/store';
let ws:WebSocket|undefined; let lastCursor:string|null=null;
export function connect(){ ws = new WebSocket(ws://${location.hostname}:8080/ws);
  ws.onopen = () => flush(); ws.onmessage = e => { const evt = JSON.parse(e.data);
    if (evt.type==='server.message.created') addMessage(evt.message.roomId, evt.message);
  }; ws.onclose = () => setTimeout(connect, 800);
}
export function sendOrQueue(payload:any){ try{ ws?.send(JSON.stringify(payload)); }catch{ enqueue({ id:payload.idempotencyKey, roomId:payload.roomId, body:payload.body, ciphertext:payload.ciphertext, idem:payload.idempotencyKey }); } }
function flush(){ for(const q of useStore.getState().queue) { ws?.send(JSON.stringify({ type:'client.message.send', roomId:q.roomId, body:q.body, ciphertext:q.ciphertext, idempotencyKey:q.idem })); dequeue(q.id); } }
E2EE helpers (sealed box via libsodium-wrappers; minimal)
tsDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
// apps/web/src/e2ee/crypto.ts
import sodium from 'libsodium-wrappers-sumo';
export async function ensureKeys(){
  await sodium.ready;
  const s = localStorage.getItem('dmKeys'); if (s) return JSON.parse(s);
  const kp = sodium.crypto_box_keypair();
  const keys = { pub: sodium.to_base64(kp.publicKey), sec: sodium.to_base64(kp.privateKey) };
  localStorage.setItem('dmKeys', JSON.stringify(keys)); return keys;
}
export async function encryptFor(pubB64:string, text:string){
  await sodium.ready; return sodium.to_base64(sodium.crypto_box_seal(new TextEncoder().encode(text), sodium.from_base64(pubB64)));
}
export async function decryptFrom(cipherB64:string){
  await sodium.ready; const { pub, sec } = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('dmKeys')!);
  const m = sodium.crypto_box_seal_open(sodium.from_base64(cipherB64), sodium.from_base64(pub), sodium.from_base64(sec));
  return new TextDecoder().decode(m);
}
Minimal Rule Editor (WHEN contains → THEN add_task)
tsxDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
// apps/web/src/rules/RuleEditor.tsx
import React,{useState} from 'react';
export default function RuleEditor({roomId}:{roomId:string}) {
  const [contains,setContains]=useState('#todo');
  async function save(){
    await fetch(/rooms/${roomId}/rules, { method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify({ when_json:{contains}, then_json:[{add_task:{title:'Auto'}}] })});
    alert('Rule saved');
  }
  return <div><input value={contains} onChange={e=>setContains(e.target.value)}/><button onClick={save}>Save</button></div>;
}

import React from 'react';
export default function Tasks({canvas}:{canvas:any}) {
  return <div><h4>Task List</h4><ul>{(canvas.data.tasks||[]).map((t:any)=><li key={t.id}>• {t.title}</li>)}</ul></div>;
}

    depends_on: [api]

name: ci

    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: actions/setup-java@v4
        with: { distribution: temurin, java-version: '21' }
      - name: Build API
        run: cd apps/api && ./gradlew -x test bootJar
      - name: Build Web
        run: cd apps/web && npm ci && npm run build
Local run (2 commands)

* docker-compose up --build
* Open http://localhost:5173 and click “Dev Login” (simple dev auth), create a room, add rule “#todo”, send a message, see Task List update.


1. Runbook, limits, and future work (super short)


* Start/stop: docker-compose up -d / down.
* Backups: pg_dump -Fc -h localhost -U postgres orbitchat > backup.dump.
* Metrics: Spring Actuator /actuator/prometheus (scrape with Prometheus if desired).
Limits
* Dev auth only (use OAuth/JWT when expanding).
* E2EE is sealed‑box (no forward secrecy).
* Whiteboard uses last‑write‑wins ops; not a full CRDT.
Future
* JWT + OAuth2, passkeys, better S3 presign (AWS SDK), richer rules, true CRDT, full search UI.


1. Resume bullets (3) + 30‑second demo
Resume bullets


* Built OrbitChat (Java 21, Spring WebFlux, React) — programmable chat with per‑room rules and real‑time canvases (Tasks, Poll, Whiteboard), plus Time Capsules; offline‑first PWA with WebSocket backfill.
* Implemented optional E2EE for 1:1 DMs using browser X25519 sealed‑box (libsodium); server stores ciphertext only; non‑E2EE rooms searchable via Postgres FTS.
* Shipped slim, deployable MVP with Docker‑based dev, Fly‑ready images, Prometheus/Actuator metrics, and a tiny rules engine that automates task capture from chat.

30‑second demo

* “I log into OrbitChat, create a room, and add a rule: WHEN message contains ‘#todo’ THEN add to Task List. I send ‘Ship landing page #todo’ and the Tasks canvas updates instantly. I open Polls, vote live, then schedule a Time Capsule to unlock in 1 minute. In a 1:1 DM, we exchange keys, send an encrypted message (server shows ciphertext). Finally, I go offline, send a message, reconnect, and see it delivered from the queue.”

That’s the compact, portfolio‑ready version. It keeps the core magic (rules, canvases, time capsules, optional E2EE) while trimming everything else so you can stand it up quickly and iterate.

## [17:18:17] - MAGUS Council → gemini, codex, claude
Great call. Here’s a leaner “OrbitChat – Slim MVP” that keeps the differentiators and deployability, but trims the surface area and code you need to read.

1. 
Project overview and elevator pitch (short)
OrbitChat is a programmable, offline‑first chat. Each room has simple WHEN/THEN rules, plus lightweight canvases (Tasks, Polls, Mini‑Whiteboard). Time Capsules unlock by time or reactions. Optional E2EE for 1:1 DMs uses sealed‑box in the browser; non‑E2EE rooms remain searchable. Stack: Java 21 + Spring Boot WebFlux, React + TS, Postgres, Redis. Author: Ritika Singh.

2. 
Architecture diagram (compact) + explanation
+--------------------+     WS/SSE     +----------------------+
| React PWA (Vite)   |<-------------->| Spring Boot WebFlux  |
| - Rooms/Messages   |                | - REST + WebSocket   |
| - Rule Editor      |                | - Rules Engine (MVP) |
| - Canvases (3)     |                | - Time Capsules      |
| - E2EE in browser  |                | - Presign S3         |
| - IndexedDB queue  |                | - Prometheus/Otel    |
+--------------------+                +-----+-----------+----+
| REST                               |           |
v                                     v           v
Web Push/SW                             Postgres      Redis
(core data)   (presence/pubsub)
Explanation



* WebSocket for realtime; SSE fallback.
* Offline queue flushes on reconnect with idempotency keys.
* E2EE DMs: client encrypts; server stores ciphertext only.

2. 
Database schema and Flyway migrations (first migration)
Essential tables only (presence history omitted to stay small; live presence via Redis).


sqlDownloadCopy code Wrap-- Author: Ritika Singh
-- apps/api/src/main/resources/db/migration/V1__init.sql
CREATE TYPE room_type AS ENUM ('dm','group');
CREATE TYPE role_type AS ENUM ('owner','admin','member');
CREATE TYPE canvas_type AS ENUM ('tasks','poll','whiteboard');

CREATE TABLE users (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  handle TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
  display_name TEXT NOT NULL,
  email TEXT UNIQUE,
  dm_public_key BYTEA,       -- for E2EE DMs (optional)
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

CREATE TABLE rooms (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  type room_type NOT NULL,
  name TEXT,
  created_by UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

CREATE TABLE memberships (
  user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  room_id UUID REFERENCES rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  role role_type NOT NULL,
  joined_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  PRIMARY KEY (user_id, room_id)
);

CREATE TABLE messages (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  room_id UUID REFERENCES rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  sender_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  body TEXT,
  body_ciphertext BYTEA,
  attachments JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT '[]',
  idempotency_key TEXT UNIQUE,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

CREATE TABLE rules (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  room_id UUID REFERENCES rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  when_json JSONB NOT NULL,
  then_json JSONB NOT NULL,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

CREATE TABLE canvases (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  room_id UUID REFERENCES rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  type canvas_type NOT NULL,
  data_json JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
  updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

CREATE TABLE reactions (
  message_id UUID REFERENCES messages(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  emoji TEXT NOT NULL,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  PRIMARY KEY (message_id, user_id, emoji)
);

CREATE TABLE time_capsules (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  room_id UUID REFERENCES rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  payload_json JSONB NOT NULL,             -- message to emit
  unlock_at TIMESTAMPTZ,                   -- time-based
  min_reactions INT,                       -- reaction-based
  message_id UUID,                         -- optional: associated message to watch
  unlocked_at TIMESTAMPTZ
);

-- FTS for searchable (non-E2EE) messages
CREATE MATERIALIZED VIEW fts_messages AS
SELECT id, room_id, to_tsvector('english', coalesce(body,'')) AS tsv
FROM messages WHERE body IS NOT NULL;
CREATE UNIQUE INDEX fts_messages_pk ON fts_messages (id);
CREATE INDEX fts_messages_tsv_idx ON fts_messages USING GIN (tsv);

1. Realtime protocol and message shapes (condensed)


* Transport: WebSocket /ws (JSON). SSE fallback: GET /sse (server push) + REST POST for send.
* At-least-once delivery. Client supplies idempotencyKey; server echoes it.

Client → Server

* client.message.send { roomId, body? | ciphertext?, idempotencyKey }
* client.canvas.patch { canvasId, patch, baseVersion }
* client.rule.create { roomId, when, then }
* client.typing { roomId, state }
* resume { lastCursor }

Server → Client

* server.welcome { sessionId, heartbeatSec }
* server.message.created { message, cursor }
* server.canvas.updated { canvasId, patch, version }
* server.rule.fired { ruleId, summary }
* server.timecapsule.unlocked { roomId, message }

Rule JSON (MVP)

* when: { contains:"#todo" } or { mention:"@urgent" }
* then: [ { add_task:{ title:"Auto: ${message}" } }, { pin_message:{} } ]


1. Backend (trimmed, runnable excerpts)

SecurityConfig.java (permit dev login header; JWT optional)
javaDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
package com.oc.config;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.*;
import org.springframework.security.config.annotation.web.reactive.EnableWebFluxSecurity;
import org.springframework.security.config.web.server.ServerHttpSecurity;
import org.springframework.security.web.server.SecurityWebFilterChain;
@Configuration @EnableWebFluxSecurity
public class SecurityConfig {
  @Bean SecurityWebFilterChain chain(ServerHttpSecurity http) {
    return http.csrf(csrf->csrf.disable())
      .authorizeExchange(e->e.pathMatchers("/actuator/","/ws","/sse").permitAll().anyExchange().permitAll())
      .build(); // keep simple for MVP; swap to JWT in prod
  }
}
RealtimeHandler.java (core send + broadcast + rule hook)
javaDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
package com.oc.ws;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.oc.domain.Message;
import com.oc.repo.MessageRepo;
import com.oc.rules.RuleEngine;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
import org.springframework.web.reactive.socket.*;
import reactor.core.publisher.*;
import java.util.Map;
@Component
public class RealtimeHandler implements WebSocketHandler {
  private final ObjectMapper om = new ObjectMapper();
  private final Sinks.Many<String> bus = Sinks.many().multicast().onBackpressureBuffer();
  private final MessageRepo messages; private final RuleEngine rules;
  public RealtimeHandler(MessageRepo m, RuleEngine r){ this.messages=m; this.rules=r; }
  @Override public Mono<Void> handle(WebSocketSession s) {
    var in = s.receive().map(WebSocketMessage::getPayloadAsText).flatMap(txt -> {
      try { var e = om.readValue(txt, Map.class);
        if ("client.message.send".equals(e.get("type"))) {
          var m = Message.create(e); messages.save(m); rules.onMessageCreated(m);
          bus.tryEmitNext(om.writeValueAsString(Map.of("type","server.message.created","message",m)));
        }
      } catch(Exception ignore){}
      return Mono.empty();
    });
    var out = bus.asFlux().map(s::textMessage)
      .mergeWith(Mono.just(s.textMessage("{\"type\":\"server.welcome\",\"heartbeatSec\":25}")));
    return s.send(out).and(in);
  }
}
RuleEngine.java (WHEN contains -> THEN add_task)
javaDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
package com.oc.rules;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.*;
import com.oc.domain.*;
import com.oc.repo.*;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
@Service
public class RuleEngine {
  private final RuleRepo rr; private final CanvasRepo cr; private final ObjectMapper om = new ObjectMapper();
  public RuleEngine(RuleRepo rr, CanvasRepo cr){ this.rr=rr; this.cr=cr; }
  public void onMessageCreated(Message m){
    rr.findByRoomId(m.getRoomId()).forEach(r -> {
      try {
        var when = om.readTree(r.getWhenJson()); var then = om.readTree(r.getThenJson());
        if (matches(when, m.getBody())) apply(then, m);
      } catch(Exception ignore){}
    });
  }
  private boolean matches(JsonNode w, String body){ if (body==null) return false;
    if (w.has("contains")) return body.contains(w.get("contains").asText());
    if (w.has("mention")) return body.contains(w.get("mention").asText());
    return false;
  }
  private void apply(JsonNode t, Message m){
    if (t.isArray()) t.forEach(n->apply(n,m));
    else if (t.has("add_task")) cr.addTask(m.getRoomId(), m.getBody());
    else if (t.has("pin_message")) m.setPinned(true);
  }
}
TimeCapsuleService.java (time and reaction unlock, minimal)
javaDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
package com.oc.timecapsules;
import com.oc.repo.TimeCapsuleRepo; import com.oc.domain.TimeCapsule;
import org.springframework.scheduling.annotation.Scheduled; import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
import java.time.Instant;
@Service
public class TimeCapsuleService {
  private final TimeCapsuleRepo repo;
  public TimeCapsuleService(TimeCapsuleRepo r){ this.repo=r; }
  @Scheduled(fixedDelay = 60000)
  public void tick(){
    var now = Instant.now();
    repo.findLockable(now).forEach(tc -> { tc.setUnlockedAt(now); repo.save(tc); /* emit system message */});
  }
  public void onReactionAdded(java.util.UUID messageId){
    repo.findByMessageId(messageId).ifPresent(tc -> {
      if (repo.reactionCount(messageId) >= tc.getMinReactions()) { tc.setUnlockedAt(Instant.now()); repo.save(tc); }
    });
  }
}
S3 presign controller (unchanged pattern, few lines)
javaDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
package com.oc.storage;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.*; record PresignReq(String key,String mime){} record PresignRes(String putUrl,String getUrl){}
@RestController @RequestMapping("/files")
public class S3Controller {
  @PostMapping("/presign") public PresignRes presign(@RequestBody PresignReq r){
    return new PresignRes("http://minio/put/"+r.key(),"http://minio/get/"+r.key()); // stub for MVP; swap to AWS SDK in prod
  }
}

1. Frontend (tiny but functional)

State store with offline queue
tsDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
// apps/web/src/state/store.ts
import create from 'zustand';
type Q = { id:string; roomId:string; body?:string; ciphertext?:string; idem:string };
export const useStore = create<any>(()=>({ rooms:[], messages:{}, queue:[] }));
export const addMessage = (roomId:string, msg:any) =>
  useStore.setState((s:any)=>({ messages:{...s.messages, [roomId]:[...(s.messages[roomId]||[]), msg] }}));
export const enqueue = (q:Q)=>useStore.setState((s:any)=>({ queue:[...s.queue,q] }));
export const dequeue = (id:string)=>useStore.setState((s:any)=>({ queue:s.queue.filter((x:Q)=>x.id!==id) }));
WebSocket client with resume + queue flush
tsDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
// apps/web/src/ws/realtime.ts
import { addMessage, enqueue, dequeue, useStore } from '../state/store';
let ws:WebSocket|undefined; let lastCursor:string|null=null;
export function connect(){ ws = new WebSocket(ws://${location.hostname}:8080/ws);
  ws.onopen = () => flush(); ws.onmessage = e => { const evt = JSON.parse(e.data);
    if (evt.type==='server.message.created') addMessage(evt.message.roomId, evt.message);
  }; ws.onclose = () => setTimeout(connect, 800);
}
export function sendOrQueue(payload:any){ try{ ws?.send(JSON.stringify(payload)); }catch{ enqueue({ id:payload.idempotencyKey, roomId:payload.roomId, body:payload.body, ciphertext:payload.ciphertext, idem:payload.idempotencyKey }); } }
function flush(){ for(const q of useStore.getState().queue) { ws?.send(JSON.stringify({ type:'client.message.send', roomId:q.roomId, body:q.body, ciphertext:q.ciphertext, idempotencyKey:q.idem })); dequeue(q.id); } }
E2EE helpers (sealed box via libsodium-wrappers; minimal)
tsDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
// apps/web/src/e2ee/crypto.ts
import sodium from 'libsodium-wrappers-sumo';
export async function ensureKeys(){
  await sodium.ready;
  const s = localStorage.getItem('dmKeys'); if (s) return JSON.parse(s);
  const kp = sodium.crypto_box_keypair();
  const keys = { pub: sodium.to_base64(kp.publicKey), sec: sodium.to_base64(kp.privateKey) };
  localStorage.setItem('dmKeys', JSON.stringify(keys)); return keys;
}
export async function encryptFor(pubB64:string, text:string){
  await sodium.ready; return sodium.to_base64(sodium.crypto_box_seal(new TextEncoder().encode(text), sodium.from_base64(pubB64)));
}
export async function decryptFrom(cipherB64:string){
  await sodium.ready; const { pub, sec } = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('dmKeys')!);
  const m = sodium.crypto_box_seal_open(sodium.from_base64(cipherB64), sodium.from_base64(pub), sodium.from_base64(sec));
  return new TextDecoder().decode(m);
}
Minimal Rule Editor (WHEN contains → THEN add_task)
tsxDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
// apps/web/src/rules/RuleEditor.tsx
import React,{useState} from 'react';
export default function RuleEditor({roomId}:{roomId:string}) {
  const [contains,setContains]=useState('#todo');
  async function save(){
    await fetch(/rooms/${roomId}/rules, { method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify({ when_json:{contains}, then_json:[{add_task:{title:'Auto'}}] })});
    alert('Rule saved');
  }
  return <div><input value={contains} onChange={e=>setContains(e.target.value)}/><button onClick={save}>Save</button></div>;
}

}

1. Runbook, limits, and future work (super short)


* Start/stop: docker-compose up -d / down.
* Backups: pg_dump -Fc -h localhost -U postgres orbitchat > backup.dump.
* Metrics: Spring Actuator /actuator/prometheus (scrape with Prometheus if desired).
Limits
* Dev auth only (use OAuth/JWT when expanding).
* E2EE is sealed‑box (no forward secrecy).
* Whiteboard uses last‑write‑wins ops; not a full CRDT.
Future
* JWT + OAuth2, passkeys, better S3 presign (AWS SDK), richer rules, true CRDT, full search UI.


1. Resume bullets (3) + 30‑second demo
Resume bullets


* Built OrbitChat (Java 21, Spring WebFlux, React) — programmable chat with per‑room rules and real‑time canvases (Tasks, Poll, Whiteboard), plus Time Capsules; offline‑first PWA with WebSocket backfill.
* Implemented optional E2EE for 1:1 DMs using browser X25519 sealed‑box (libsodium); server stores ciphertext only; non‑E2EE rooms searchable via Postgres FTS.
* Shipped slim, deployable MVP with Docker‑based dev, Fly‑ready images, Prometheus/Actuator metrics, and a tiny rules engine that automates task capture from chat.

30‑second demo

* “I log into OrbitChat, create a room, and add a rule: WHEN message contains ‘#todo’ THEN add to Task List. I send ‘Ship landing page #todo’ and the Tasks canvas updates instantly. I open Polls, vote live, then schedule a Time Capsule to unlock in 1 minute. In a 1:1 DM, we exchange keys, send an encrypted message (server shows ciphertext). Finally, I go offline, send a message, reconnect, and see it delivered from the queue.”

That’s the compact, portfolio‑ready version. It keeps the core magic (rules, canvases, time capsules, optional E2EE) while trimming everything else so you can stand it up quickly and iterate.

## [17:18:18] - MAGUS Council → gemini, codex, claude
Great call. Here’s a leaner “OrbitChat – Slim MVP” that keeps the differentiators and deployability, but trims the surface area and code you need to read.

1. 
Project overview and elevator pitch (short)
OrbitChat is a programmable, offline‑first chat. Each room has simple WHEN/THEN rules, plus lightweight canvases (Tasks, Polls, Mini‑Whiteboard). Time Capsules unlock by time or reactions. Optional E2EE for 1:1 DMs uses sealed‑box in the browser; non‑E2EE rooms remain searchable. Stack: Java 21 + Spring Boot WebFlux, React + TS, Postgres, Redis. Author: Ritika Singh.

2. 
Architecture diagram (compact) + explanation
+--------------------+     WS/SSE     +----------------------+
| React PWA (Vite)   |<-------------->| Spring Boot WebFlux  |
| - Rooms/Messages   |                | - REST + WebSocket   |
| - Rule Editor      |                | - Rules Engine (MVP) |
| - Canvases (3)     |                | - Time Capsules      |
| - E2EE in browser  |                | - Presign S3         |
| - IndexedDB queue  |                | - Prometheus/Otel    |
+--------------------+                +-----+-----------+----+
| REST                               |           |
v                                     v           v
Web Push/SW                             Postgres      Redis
(core data)   (presence/pubsub)
Explanation



* WebSocket for realtime; SSE fallback.
* Offline queue flushes on reconnect with idempotency keys.
* E2EE DMs: client encrypts; server stores ciphertext only.

2. 
Database schema and Flyway migrations (first migration)
Essential tables only (presence history omitted to stay small; live presence via Redis).


sqlDownloadCopy code Wrap-- Author: Ritika Singh
-- apps/api/src/main/resources/db/migration/V1__init.sql
CREATE TYPE room_type AS ENUM ('dm','group');
CREATE TYPE role_type AS ENUM ('owner','admin','member');
CREATE TYPE canvas_type AS ENUM ('tasks','poll','whiteboard');

CREATE TABLE users (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  handle TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
  display_name TEXT NOT NULL,
  email TEXT UNIQUE,
  dm_public_key BYTEA,       -- for E2EE DMs (optional)
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

CREATE TABLE rooms (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  type room_type NOT NULL,
  name TEXT,
  created_by UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

CREATE TABLE memberships (
  user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  room_id UUID REFERENCES rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  role role_type NOT NULL,
  joined_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  PRIMARY KEY (user_id, room_id)
);

CREATE TABLE messages (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  room_id UUID REFERENCES rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  sender_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  body TEXT,
  body_ciphertext BYTEA,
  attachments JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT '[]',
  idempotency_key TEXT UNIQUE,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

CREATE TABLE rules (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  room_id UUID REFERENCES rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  when_json JSONB NOT NULL,
  then_json JSONB NOT NULL,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

CREATE TABLE canvases (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  room_id UUID REFERENCES rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  type canvas_type NOT NULL,
  data_json JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
  updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

CREATE TABLE reactions (
  message_id UUID REFERENCES messages(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  emoji TEXT NOT NULL,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  PRIMARY KEY (message_id, user_id, emoji)
);

CREATE TABLE time_capsules (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  room_id UUID REFERENCES rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  payload_json JSONB NOT NULL,             -- message to emit
  unlock_at TIMESTAMPTZ,                   -- time-based
  min_reactions INT,                       -- reaction-based
  message_id UUID,                         -- optional: associated message to watch
  unlocked_at TIMESTAMPTZ
);

-- FTS for searchable (non-E2EE) messages
CREATE MATERIALIZED VIEW fts_messages AS
SELECT id, room_id, to_tsvector('english', coalesce(body,'')) AS tsv
FROM messages WHERE body IS NOT NULL;
CREATE UNIQUE INDEX fts_messages_pk ON fts_messages (id);
CREATE INDEX fts_messages_tsv_idx ON fts_messages USING GIN (tsv);

import org.springframework.security.web.server.SecurityWebFilterChain;

    return http.csrf(csrf->csrf.disable())

      .build(); // keep simple for MVP; swap to JWT in prod

RealtimeHandler.java (core send + broadcast + rule hook)
javaDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
package com.oc.ws;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.oc.domain.Message;
import com.oc.repo.MessageRepo;
import com.oc.rules.RuleEngine;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
import org.springframework.web.reactive.socket.*;
import reactor.core.publisher.*;
import java.util.Map;
@Component
public class RealtimeHandler implements WebSocketHandler {
  private final ObjectMapper om = new ObjectMapper();
  private final Sinks.Many<String> bus = Sinks.many().multicast().onBackpressureBuffer();
  private final MessageRepo messages; private final RuleEngine rules;
  public RealtimeHandler(MessageRepo m, RuleEngine r){ this.messages=m; this.rules=r; }
  @Override public Mono<Void> handle(WebSocketSession s) {
    var in = s.receive().map(WebSocketMessage::getPayloadAsText).flatMap(txt -> {
      try { var e = om.readValue(txt, Map.class);
        if ("client.message.send".equals(e.get("type"))) {
          var m = Message.create(e); messages.save(m); rules.onMessageCreated(m);
          bus.tryEmitNext(om.writeValueAsString(Map.of("type","server.message.created","message",m)));
        }
      } catch(Exception ignore){}
      return Mono.empty();
    });
    var out = bus.asFlux().map(s::textMessage)
      .mergeWith(Mono.just(s.textMessage("{\"type\":\"server.welcome\",\"heartbeatSec\":25}")));
    return s.send(out).and(in);
  }
}
RuleEngine.java (WHEN contains -> THEN add_task)
javaDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
package com.oc.rules;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.*;
import com.oc.domain.*;
import com.oc.repo.*;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
@Service
public class RuleEngine {
  private final RuleRepo rr; private final CanvasRepo cr; private final ObjectMapper om = new ObjectMapper();
  public RuleEngine(RuleRepo rr, CanvasRepo cr){ this.rr=rr; this.cr=cr; }
  public void onMessageCreated(Message m){
    rr.findByRoomId(m.getRoomId()).forEach(r -> {
      try {
        var when = om.readTree(r.getWhenJson()); var then = om.readTree(r.getThenJson());
        if (matches(when, m.getBody())) apply(then, m);
      } catch(Exception ignore){}
    });
  }
  private boolean matches(JsonNode w, String body){ if (body==null) return false;
    if (w.has("contains")) return body.contains(w.get("contains").asText());
    if (w.has("mention")) return body.contains(w.get("mention").asText());
    return false;
  }
  private void apply(JsonNode t, Message m){
    if (t.isArray()) t.forEach(n->apply(n,m));
    else if (t.has("add_task")) cr.addTask(m.getRoomId(), m.getBody());
    else if (t.has("pin_message")) m.setPinned(true);
  }
}
TimeCapsuleService.java (time and reaction unlock, minimal)
javaDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
package com.oc.timecapsules;
import com.oc.repo.TimeCapsuleRepo; import com.oc.domain.TimeCapsule;
import org.springframework.scheduling.annotation.Scheduled; import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
import java.time.Instant;
@Service
public class TimeCapsuleService {
  private final TimeCapsuleRepo repo;
  public TimeCapsuleService(TimeCapsuleRepo r){ this.repo=r; }
  @Scheduled(fixedDelay = 60000)
  public void tick(){
    var now = Instant.now();
    repo.findLockable(now).forEach(tc -> { tc.setUnlockedAt(now); repo.save(tc); /* emit system message */});
  }
  public void onReactionAdded(java.util.UUID messageId){
    repo.findByMessageId(messageId).ifPresent(tc -> {
      if (repo.reactionCount(messageId) >= tc.getMinReactions()) { tc.setUnlockedAt(Instant.now()); repo.save(tc); }
    });
  }
}

1. Frontend (tiny but functional)

State store with offline queue
tsDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
// apps/web/src/state/store.ts
import create from 'zustand';
type Q = { id:string; roomId:string; body?:string; ciphertext?:string; idem:string };
export const useStore = create<any>(()=>({ rooms:[], messages:{}, queue:[] }));
export const addMessage = (roomId:string, msg:any) =>
  useStore.setState((s:any)=>({ messages:{...s.messages, [roomId]:[...(s.messages[roomId]||[]), msg] }}));
export const enqueue = (q:Q)=>useStore.setState((s:any)=>({ queue:[...s.queue,q] }));
export const dequeue = (id:string)=>useStore.setState((s:any)=>({ queue:s.queue.filter((x:Q)=>x.id!==id) }));
WebSocket client with resume + queue flush
tsDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
// apps/web/src/ws/realtime.ts
import { addMessage, enqueue, dequeue, useStore } from '../state/store';
let ws:WebSocket|undefined; let lastCursor:string|null=null;
export function connect(){ ws = new WebSocket(ws://${location.hostname}:8080/ws);
  ws.onopen = () => flush(); ws.onmessage = e => { const evt = JSON.parse(e.data);
    if (evt.type==='server.message.created') addMessage(evt.message.roomId, evt.message);
  }; ws.onclose = () => setTimeout(connect, 800);
}
export function sendOrQueue(payload:any){ try{ ws?.send(JSON.stringify(payload)); }catch{ enqueue({ id:payload.idempotencyKey, roomId:payload.roomId, body:payload.body, ciphertext:payload.ciphertext, idem:payload.idempotencyKey }); } }
function flush(){ for(const q of useStore.getState().queue) { ws?.send(JSON.stringify({ type:'client.message.send', roomId:q.roomId, body:q.body, ciphertext:q.ciphertext, idempotencyKey:q.idem })); dequeue(q.id); } }
E2EE helpers (sealed box via libsodium-wrappers; minimal)
tsDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
// apps/web/src/e2ee/crypto.ts
import sodium from 'libsodium-wrappers-sumo';
export async function ensureKeys(){
  await sodium.ready;
  const s = localStorage.getItem('dmKeys'); if (s) return JSON.parse(s);
  const kp = sodium.crypto_box_keypair();
  const keys = { pub: sodium.to_base64(kp.publicKey), sec: sodium.to_base64(kp.privateKey) };
  localStorage.setItem('dmKeys', JSON.stringify(keys)); return keys;
}
export async function encryptFor(pubB64:string, text:string){
  await sodium.ready; return sodium.to_base64(sodium.crypto_box_seal(new TextEncoder().encode(text), sodium.from_base64(pubB64)));
}
export async function decryptFrom(cipherB64:string){
  await sodium.ready; const { pub, sec } = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('dmKeys')!);
  const m = sodium.crypto_box_seal_open(sodium.from_base64(cipherB64), sodium.from_base64(pub), sodium.from_base64(sec));
  return new TextDecoder().decode(m);
}
Minimal Rule Editor (WHEN contains → THEN add_task)
tsxDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
// apps/web/src/rules/RuleEditor.tsx
import React,{useState} from 'react';
export default function RuleEditor({roomId}:{roomId:string}) {
  const [contains,setContains]=useState('#todo');
  async function save(){
    await fetch(/rooms/${roomId}/rules, { method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify({ when_json:{contains}, then_json:[{add_task:{title:'Auto'}}] })});
    alert('Rule saved');
  }
  return <div><input value={contains} onChange={e=>setContains(e.target.value)}/><button onClick={save}>Save</button></div>;
}

1. Runbook, limits, and future work (super short)


* Start/stop: docker-compose up -d / down.
* Backups: pg_dump -Fc -h localhost -U postgres orbitchat > backup.dump.
* Metrics: Spring Actuator /actuator/prometheus (scrape with Prometheus if desired).
Limits
* Dev auth only (use OAuth/JWT when expanding).
* E2EE is sealed‑box (no forward secrecy).
* Whiteboard uses last‑write‑wins ops; not a full CRDT.
Future
* JWT + OAuth2, passkeys, better S3 presign (AWS SDK), richer rules, true CRDT, full search UI.


1. Resume bullets (3) + 30‑second demo
Resume bullets


* Built OrbitChat (Java 21, Spring WebFlux, React) — programmable chat with per‑room rules and real‑time canvases (Tasks, Poll, Whiteboard), plus Time Capsules; offline‑first PWA with WebSocket backfill.
* Implemented optional E2EE for 1:1 DMs using browser X25519 sealed‑box (libsodium); server stores ciphertext only; non‑E2EE rooms searchable via Postgres FTS.
* Shipped slim, deployable MVP with Docker‑based dev, Fly‑ready images, Prometheus/Actuator metrics, and a tiny rules engine that automates task capture from chat.

30‑second demo

* “I log into OrbitChat, create a room, and add a rule: WHEN message contains ‘#todo’ THEN add to Task List. I send ‘Ship landing page #todo’ and the Tasks canvas updates instantly. I open Polls, vote live, then schedule a Time Capsule to unlock in 1 minute. In a 1:1 DM, we exchange keys, send an encrypted message (server shows ciphertext). Finally, I go offline, send a message, reconnect, and see it delivered from the queue.”

That’s the compact, portfolio‑ready version. It keeps the core magic (rules, canvases, time capsules, optional E2EE) while trimming everything else so you can stand it up quickly and iterate.

## [17:18:21] - MAGUS Council → codex
Great call. Here’s a leaner “OrbitChat – Slim MVP” that keeps the differentiators and deployability, but trims the surface area and code you need to read.

1. 
Project overview and elevator pitch (short)
OrbitChat is a programmable, offline‑first chat. Each room has simple WHEN/THEN rules, plus lightweight canvases (Tasks, Polls, Mini‑Whiteboard). Time Capsules unlock by time or reactions. Optional E2EE for 1:1 DMs uses sealed‑box in the browser; non‑E2EE rooms remain searchable. Stack: Java 21 + Spring Boot WebFlux, React + TS, Postgres, Redis. Author: Ritika Singh.

2. 
Architecture diagram (compact) + explanation
+--------------------+     WS/SSE     +----------------------+
| React PWA (Vite)   |<-------------->| Spring Boot WebFlux  |
| - Rooms/Messages   |                | - REST + WebSocket   |
| - Rule Editor      |                | - Rules Engine (MVP) |
| - Canvases (3)     |                | - Time Capsules      |
| - E2EE in browser  |                | - Presign S3         |
| - IndexedDB queue  |                | - Prometheus/Otel    |
+--------------------+                +-----+-----------+----+
| REST                               |           |
v                                     v           v
Web Push/SW                             Postgres      Redis
(core data)   (presence/pubsub)
Explanation



* WebSocket for realtime; SSE fallback.
* Offline queue flushes on reconnect with idempotency keys.
* E2EE DMs: client encrypts; server stores ciphertext only.

2. 
Database schema and Flyway migrations (first migration)
Essential tables only (presence history omitted to stay small; live presence via Redis).


sqlDownloadCopy code Wrap-- Author: Ritika Singh
-- apps/api/src/main/resources/db/migration/V1__init.sql
CREATE TYPE room_type AS ENUM ('dm','group');
CREATE TYPE role_type AS ENUM ('owner','admin','member');
CREATE TYPE canvas_type AS ENUM ('tasks','poll','whiteboard');

CREATE TABLE users (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  handle TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
  display_name TEXT NOT NULL,
  email TEXT UNIQUE,
  dm_public_key BYTEA,       -- for E2EE DMs (optional)
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

CREATE TABLE rooms (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  type room_type NOT NULL,
  name TEXT,
  created_by UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

CREATE TABLE memberships (
  user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  room_id UUID REFERENCES rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  role role_type NOT NULL,
  joined_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  PRIMARY KEY (user_id, room_id)
);

CREATE TABLE messages (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  room_id UUID REFERENCES rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  sender_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  body TEXT,
  body_ciphertext BYTEA,
  attachments JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT '[]',
  idempotency_key TEXT UNIQUE,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

CREATE TABLE rules (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  room_id UUID REFERENCES rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  when_json JSONB NOT NULL,
  then_json JSONB NOT NULL,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

CREATE TABLE canvases (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  room_id UUID REFERENCES rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  type canvas_type NOT NULL,
  data_json JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
  updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

CREATE TABLE reactions (
  message_id UUID REFERENCES messages(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  emoji TEXT NOT NULL,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  PRIMARY KEY (message_id, user_id, emoji)
);

CREATE TABLE time_capsules (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  room_id UUID REFERENCES rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  payload_json JSONB NOT NULL,             -- message to emit
  unlock_at TIMESTAMPTZ,                   -- time-based
  min_reactions INT,                       -- reaction-based
  message_id UUID,                         -- optional: associated message to watch
  unlocked_at TIMESTAMPTZ
);

-- FTS for searchable (non-E2EE) messages
CREATE MATERIALIZED VIEW fts_messages AS
SELECT id, room_id, to_tsvector('english', coalesce(body,'')) AS tsv
FROM messages WHERE body IS NOT NULL;
CREATE UNIQUE INDEX fts_messages_pk ON fts_messages (id);
CREATE INDEX fts_messages_tsv_idx ON fts_messages USING GIN (tsv);

paths:

  /rooms:
    get: { summary: List rooms }
    post: { summary: Create room }
  /rooms/{id}/messages:
    get: { summary: List with cursor }
    post: { summary: Send (plaintext or ciphertext) }
  /rooms/{id}/rules:
    get: { summary: List rules }

  /rooms/{id}/canvases:

    post: { summary: Create canvas }
  /canvases/{id}: { patch: { summary: Patch data_json } }
  /dm-keys:
    post: { summary: Set my public key (base64) }
  /dm-keys/{userId}:
    get: { summary: Get user’s public key }
  /search: { get: { summary: FTS (non‑E2EE) } }
  /files/presign: { post: { summary: S3 presigned URLs } }

security: [ { bearerAuth: [] } ]

1. Realtime protocol and message shapes (condensed)


* Transport: WebSocket /ws (JSON). SSE fallback: GET /sse (server push) + REST POST for send.
* At-least-once delivery. Client supplies idempotencyKey; server echoes it.

Client → Server

* client.message.send { roomId, body? | ciphertext?, idempotencyKey }
* client.canvas.patch { canvasId, patch, baseVersion }
* client.rule.create { roomId, when, then }
* client.typing { roomId, state }
* resume { lastCursor }

Server → Client

* server.welcome { sessionId, heartbeatSec }
* server.message.created { message, cursor }
* server.canvas.updated { canvasId, patch, version }
* server.rule.fired { ruleId, summary }
* server.timecapsule.unlocked { roomId, message }

Rule JSON (MVP)

* when: { contains:"#todo" } or { mention:"@urgent" }
* then: [ { add_task:{ title:"Auto: ${message}" } }, { pin_message:{} } ]


1. Backend (trimmed, runnable excerpts)

SecurityConfig.java (permit dev login header; JWT optional)
javaDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
package com.oc.config;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.*;
import org.springframework.security.config.annotation.web.reactive.EnableWebFluxSecurity;
import org.springframework.security.config.web.server.ServerHttpSecurity;
import org.springframework.security.web.server.SecurityWebFilterChain;
@Configuration @EnableWebFluxSecurity
public class SecurityConfig {
  @Bean SecurityWebFilterChain chain(ServerHttpSecurity http) {
    return http.csrf(csrf->csrf.disable())
      .authorizeExchange(e->e.pathMatchers("/actuator/","/ws","/sse").permitAll().anyExchange().permitAll())
      .build(); // keep simple for MVP; swap to JWT in prod
  }
}
RealtimeHandler.java (core send + broadcast + rule hook)
javaDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
package com.oc.ws;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.oc.domain.Message;
import com.oc.repo.MessageRepo;
import com.oc.rules.RuleEngine;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
import org.springframework.web.reactive.socket.*;
import reactor.core.publisher.*;
import java.util.Map;
@Component
public class RealtimeHandler implements WebSocketHandler {
  private final ObjectMapper om = new ObjectMapper();
  private final Sinks.Many<String> bus = Sinks.many().multicast().onBackpressureBuffer();
  private final MessageRepo messages; private final RuleEngine rules;
  public RealtimeHandler(MessageRepo m, RuleEngine r){ this.messages=m; this.rules=r; }
  @Override public Mono<Void> handle(WebSocketSession s) {
    var in = s.receive().map(WebSocketMessage::getPayloadAsText).flatMap(txt -> {
      try { var e = om.readValue(txt, Map.class);
        if ("client.message.send".equals(e.get("type"))) {
          var m = Message.create(e); messages.save(m); rules.onMessageCreated(m);
          bus.tryEmitNext(om.writeValueAsString(Map.of("type","server.message.created","message",m)));
        }
      } catch(Exception ignore){}
      return Mono.empty();
    });
    var out = bus.asFlux().map(s::textMessage)
      .mergeWith(Mono.just(s.textMessage("{\"type\":\"server.welcome\",\"heartbeatSec\":25}")));
    return s.send(out).and(in);
  }
}
RuleEngine.java (WHEN contains -> THEN add_task)
javaDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
package com.oc.rules;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.*;
import com.oc.domain.*;
import com.oc.repo.*;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
@Service
public class RuleEngine {
  private final RuleRepo rr; private final CanvasRepo cr; private final ObjectMapper om = new ObjectMapper();
  public RuleEngine(RuleRepo rr, CanvasRepo cr){ this.rr=rr; this.cr=cr; }
  public void onMessageCreated(Message m){
    rr.findByRoomId(m.getRoomId()).forEach(r -> {
      try {
        var when = om.readTree(r.getWhenJson()); var then = om.readTree(r.getThenJson());
        if (matches(when, m.getBody())) apply(then, m);
      } catch(Exception ignore){}
    });
  }
  private boolean matches(JsonNode w, String body){ if (body==null) return false;
    if (w.has("contains")) return body.contains(w.get("contains").asText());
    if (w.has("mention")) return body.contains(w.get("mention").asText());
    return false;
  }
  private void apply(JsonNode t, Message m){
    if (t.isArray()) t.forEach(n->apply(n,m));
    else if (t.has("add_task")) cr.addTask(m.getRoomId(), m.getBody());
    else if (t.has("pin_message")) m.setPinned(true);
  }
}
TimeCapsuleService.java (time and reaction unlock, minimal)
javaDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
package com.oc.timecapsules;
import com.oc.repo.TimeCapsuleRepo; import com.oc.domain.TimeCapsule;
import org.springframework.scheduling.annotation.Scheduled; import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
import java.time.Instant;
@Service
public class TimeCapsuleService {
  private final TimeCapsuleRepo repo;
  public TimeCapsuleService(TimeCapsuleRepo r){ this.repo=r; }
  @Scheduled(fixedDelay = 60000)
  public void tick(){
    var now = Instant.now();
    repo.findLockable(now).forEach(tc -> { tc.setUnlockedAt(now); repo.save(tc); /* emit system message */});
  }
  public void onReactionAdded(java.util.UUID messageId){
    repo.findByMessageId(messageId).ifPresent(tc -> {
      if (repo.reactionCount(messageId) >= tc.getMinReactions()) { tc.setUnlockedAt(Instant.now()); repo.save(tc); }
    });
  }
}

1. Frontend (tiny but functional)

State store with offline queue
tsDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
// apps/web/src/state/store.ts
import create from 'zustand';
type Q = { id:string; roomId:string; body?:string; ciphertext?:string; idem:string };
export const useStore = create<any>(()=>({ rooms:[], messages:{}, queue:[] }));
export const addMessage = (roomId:string, msg:any) =>
  useStore.setState((s:any)=>({ messages:{...s.messages, [roomId]:[...(s.messages[roomId]||[]), msg] }}));
export const enqueue = (q:Q)=>useStore.setState((s:any)=>({ queue:[...s.queue,q] }));
export const dequeue = (id:string)=>useStore.setState((s:any)=>({ queue:s.queue.filter((x:Q)=>x.id!==id) }));
WebSocket client with resume + queue flush
tsDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
// apps/web/src/ws/realtime.ts
import { addMessage, enqueue, dequeue, useStore } from '../state/store';
let ws:WebSocket|undefined; let lastCursor:string|null=null;
export function connect(){ ws = new WebSocket(ws://${location.hostname}:8080/ws);
  ws.onopen = () => flush(); ws.onmessage = e => { const evt = JSON.parse(e.data);
    if (evt.type==='server.message.created') addMessage(evt.message.roomId, evt.message);
  }; ws.onclose = () => setTimeout(connect, 800);
}
export function sendOrQueue(payload:any){ try{ ws?.send(JSON.stringify(payload)); }catch{ enqueue({ id:payload.idempotencyKey, roomId:payload.roomId, body:payload.body, ciphertext:payload.ciphertext, idem:payload.idempotencyKey }); } }
function flush(){ for(const q of useStore.getState().queue) { ws?.send(JSON.stringify({ type:'client.message.send', roomId:q.roomId, body:q.body, ciphertext:q.ciphertext, idempotencyKey:q.idem })); dequeue(q.id); } }
E2EE helpers (sealed box via libsodium-wrappers; minimal)
tsDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
// apps/web/src/e2ee/crypto.ts
import sodium from 'libsodium-wrappers-sumo';
export async function ensureKeys(){
  await sodium.ready;
  const s = localStorage.getItem('dmKeys'); if (s) return JSON.parse(s);
  const kp = sodium.crypto_box_keypair();
  const keys = { pub: sodium.to_base64(kp.publicKey), sec: sodium.to_base64(kp.privateKey) };
  localStorage.setItem('dmKeys', JSON.stringify(keys)); return keys;
}
export async function encryptFor(pubB64:string, text:string){
  await sodium.ready; return sodium.to_base64(sodium.crypto_box_seal(new TextEncoder().encode(text), sodium.from_base64(pubB64)));
}
export async function decryptFrom(cipherB64:string){
  await sodium.ready; const { pub, sec } = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('dmKeys')!);
  const m = sodium.crypto_box_seal_open(sodium.from_base64(cipherB64), sodium.from_base64(pub), sodium.from_base64(sec));
  return new TextDecoder().decode(m);
}
Minimal Rule Editor (WHEN contains → THEN add_task)
tsxDownloadCopy code Wrap// Author: Ritika Singh
// apps/web/src/rules/RuleEditor.tsx
import React,{useState} from 'react';
export default function RuleEditor({roomId}:{roomId:string}) {
  const [contains,setContains]=useState('#todo');
  async function save(){
    await fetch(/rooms/${roomId}/rules, { method:'POST', headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify({ when_json:{contains}, then_json:[{add_task:{title:'Auto'}}] })});
    alert('Rule saved');
  }
  return <div><input value={contains} onChange={e=>setContains(e.target.value)}/><button onClick={save}>Save</button></div>;
}

1. Runbook, limits, and future work (super short)


* Start/stop: docker-compose up -d / down.
* Backups: pg_dump -Fc -h localhost -U postgres orbitchat > backup.dump.
* Metrics: Spring Actuator /actuator/prometheus (scrape with Prometheus if desired).
Limits
* Dev auth only (use OAuth/JWT when expanding).
* E2EE is sealed‑box (no forward secrecy).
* Whiteboard uses last‑write‑wins ops; not a full CRDT.
Future
* JWT + OAuth2, passkeys, better S3 presign (AWS SDK), richer rules, true CRDT, full search UI.


1. Resume bullets (3) + 30‑second demo
Resume bullets


* Built OrbitChat (Java 21, Spring WebFlux, React) — programmable chat with per‑room rules and real‑time canvases (Tasks, Poll, Whiteboard), plus Time Capsules; offline‑first PWA with WebSocket backfill.
* Implemented optional E2EE for 1:1 DMs using browser X25519 sealed‑box (libsodium); server stores ciphertext only; non‑E2EE rooms searchable via Postgres FTS.
* Shipped slim, deployable MVP with Docker‑based dev, Fly‑ready images, Prometheus/Actuator metrics, and a tiny rules engine that automates task capture from chat.

30‑second demo

* “I log into OrbitChat, create a room, and add a rule: WHEN message contains ‘#todo’ THEN add to Task List. I send ‘Ship landing page #todo’ and the Tasks canvas updates instantly. I open Polls, vote live, then schedule a Time Capsule to unlock in 1 minute. In a 1:1 DM, we exchange keys, send an encrypted message (server shows ciphertext). Finally, I go offline, send a message, reconnect, and see it delivered from the queue.”

That’s the compact, portfolio‑ready version. It keeps the core magic (rules, canvases, time capsules, optional E2EE) while trimming everything else so you can stand it up quickly and iterate.

## [17:18:21] - MAGUS Council → codex
Great call. Here’s a leaner “OrbitChat – Slim MVP” that keeps the differentiators and deployability, but trims the surface area and code you need to read.

1. 
Project overview and elevator pitch (short)
OrbitChat is a programmable, offline‑first chat. Each room has simple WHEN/THEN rules, plus lightweight canvases (Tasks, Polls, Mini‑Whiteboard). Time Capsules unlock by time or reactions. Optional E2EE for 1:1 DMs uses sealed‑box in the browser; non‑E2EE rooms remain searchable. Stack: Java 21 + Spring Boot WebFlux, React + TS, Postgres, Redis. Author: Ritika Singh.

2. 
Architecture diagram (compact) + explanation
+--------------------+     WS/SSE     +----------------------+
| React PWA (Vite)   |<-------------->| Spring Boot WebFlux  |
| - Rooms/Messages   |                | - REST + WebSocket   |
| - Rule Editor      |                | - Rules Engine (MVP) |
| - Canvases (3)     |                | - Time Capsules      |
| - E2EE in browser  |                | - Presign S3         |
| - IndexedDB queue  |                | - Prometheus/Otel    |
+--------------------+                +-----+-----------+----+
| REST                               |           |
v                                     v           v
Web Push/SW                             Postgres      Redis
(core data)   (presence/pubsub)
Explanation



* WebSocket for realtime; SSE fallback.
* Offline queue flushes on reconnect with idempotency keys.
* E2EE DMs: client encrypts; server stores ciphertext only.

2. 
Database schema and Flyway migrations (first migration)
Essential tables only (presence history omitted to stay small; live presence via Redis).


sqlDownloadCopy code Wrap-- Author: Ritika Singh
-- apps/api/src/main/resources/db/migration/V1__init.sql
CREATE TYPE room_type AS ENUM ('dm','group');
CREATE TYPE role_type AS ENUM ('owner','admin','member');
CREATE TYPE canvas_type AS ENUM ('tasks','poll','whiteboard');

CREATE TABLE users (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  handle TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
  display_name TEXT NOT NULL,
  email TEXT UNIQUE,
  dm_public_key BYTEA,       -- for E2EE DMs (optional)
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

CREATE TABLE rooms (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  type room_type NOT NULL,
  name TEXT,
  created_by UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

CREATE TABLE memberships (
  user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  room_id UUID REFERENCES rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  role role_type NOT NULL,
  joined_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  PRIMARY KEY (user_id, room_id)
);

CREATE TABLE messages (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  room_id UUID REFERENCES rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  sender_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  body TEXT,
  body_ciphertext BYTEA,
  attachments JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT '[]',
  idempotency_key TEXT UNIQUE,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

CREATE TABLE rules (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  room_id UUID REFERENCES rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  when_json JSONB NOT NULL,
  then_json JSONB NOT NULL,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

CREATE TABLE canvases (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  room_id UUID REFERENCES rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  type canvas_type NOT NULL,
  data_json JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
  updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

CREATE TABLE reactions (
  message_id UUID REFERENCES messages(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  emoji TEXT NOT NULL,
  created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  PRIMARY KEY (message_id, user_id, emoji)
);

CREATE TABLE time_capsules (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
  room_id UUID REFERENCES rooms(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  payload_json JSONB NOT NULL,             -- message to emit
  unlock_at TIMESTAMPTZ,                   -- time-based
  min_reactions INT,                       -- reaction-based
  message_id UUID,                         -- optional: associated message to watch
  unlocked_at TIMESTAMPTZ
);

-- FTS for searchable (non-E2EE) messages
CREATE MATERIALIZED VIEW fts_messages AS
SELECT id, room_id, to_tsvector('english', coalesce(body,'')) AS tsv
FROM messages WHERE body IS NOT NULL;
CREATE UNIQUE INDEX fts_messages_pk ON fts_messages (id);
CREATE INDEX fts_messages_tsv_idx ON fts_messages USING GIN (tsv);

paths:

  /rooms:
    get: { summary: List rooms }
    post: { summary: Create room }
  /rooms/{id}/messages:
    get: { summary: List with cursor }
    post: { summary: Send (plaintext or ciphertext) }
  /rooms/{id}/rules:
    get: { summary: List rules }
    post: { summary: Create rule }
  /rooms/{id}/canvases:
    get: { summary: Get canvases }
    post: { summary: Create canvas }
  /canvases/{id}: { patch: { summary: Patch data_json } }
  /dm-keys:
    post: { summary: Set my public key (base64) }
  /dm-keys/{userId}:
    get: { summary: Get user’s public key }
  /search: { get: { summary: FTS (non‑E2EE) } }
  /files/presign: { post: { summary: S3 presigned URLs } }
